local Players = game:GetService("Players")
local authorList = {
"Canada00709",
"shijie2025"
}
local function isAuthor(name)
  for _, nameStr in ipairs(authorList) do
    if name == nameStr then
      return true
    end
  end
  return false
end

task.spawn(function()
while task.wait(0.5) do
  local localPlr = game.Players.LocalPlayer
  if isAuthor(localPlr.Name) then
    continue
  end
  for _, plr in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
    if isAuthor(plr.Name) then
      game.Players.LocalPlayer:Kick("检测到作者or作者朋友,已自动踢出")
      return
    end
  end
end
end)
